#This is all the data needed to calculate the monthly seroprevalence as analysed in the main article. Each line corresponds to an individual Mastomys natalensis that was captured in the field in Morogoro (Tanzania). Although not used in this article, information about the individual sex, body weight, reproductive and recapture state is available upon reasonable request (email: herwig.leirs@uantwerpen.be).
